whatsapp_api.py
```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI
class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"
    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")
    def receive_message(self, message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(message)
        return response
```

chatgpt_api.py
```python
'''
Interfaces with the OpenAI ChatGPT API for intelligent conversation.
'''
import os
import openai
class ChatGPTAPI:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        '''
        Initializes the ChatGPTAPI with the provided OpenAI API key.
        Parameters:
        api_key (str): The API key for authenticating with OpenAI.
        '''
        self.api_key = api_key
        openai.api_key = self.api_key
    def get_response(self, prompt):
        '''
        Gets a response from the ChatGPT model based on the provided prompt.
        Parameters:
        prompt (str): The input text to which the model should respond.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by the ChatGPT model.
        '''
        try:
            response = openai.Completion.create(
                engine="text-davinci-003",
                prompt=prompt,
                max_tokens=150
            )
            return response.choices[0].text.strip()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to get response from ChatGPT: {e}")
            return "Sorry, I'm having trouble understanding you right now."
```

database.py
```python
'''
Manages database operations for customer registration and booking.
'''
import sqlite3
class DatabaseManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.connection = sqlite3.connect('chatbot.db')
        self.create_tables()
    def create_tables(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                phone TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER,
                service TEXT NOT NULL,
                date TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)
            )
        ''')
        self.connection.commit()
    def register_customer(self, customer_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO customers (name, phone) VALUES (?, ?)
        ''', (customer_data['name'], customer_data['phone']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def book_service(self, booking_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)
        ''', (booking_data['customer_id'], booking_data['service'], booking_data['date']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def get_bookings(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM bookings')
        return cursor.fetchall()
```

notifications.py
```python
'''
Handles notification features for the application.
'''
import os
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.smtp_server = os.getenv("SMTP_SERVER")
        self.smtp_port = os.getenv("SMTP_PORT")
        self.smtp_user = os.getenv("SMTP_USER")
        self.smtp_password = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD")
    def send_notification(self, user_email, subject, message):
        '''
        Sends a notification to the specified user with the given message.
        Parameters:
        user_email (str): The recipient's email address.
        subject (str): The subject of the email.
        message (str): The message content of the email.
        '''
        try:
            # Set up the server
            server = smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port)
            server.starttls()
            server.login(self.smtp_user, self.smtp_password)
            # Create the email
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.smtp_user
            msg['To'] = user_email
            msg['Subject'] = subject
            msg.attach(MIMEText(message, 'plain'))
            # Send the email
            server.sendmail(self.smtp_user, user_email, msg.as_string())
            server.quit()
            print(f"Notification sent to {user_email}: {subject}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send notification: {e}")
```

whatsapp_api.py
```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from flask import Flask, request
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI

class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"

    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")

    def receive_message(self, incoming_message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        incoming_message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(incoming_message)
        return response

# Flask app for webhook
app = Flask(__name__)
whatsapp_api = WhatsAppAPI(phone_number_id=os.getenv("WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"))

@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])
def webhook():
    '''
    Webhook endpoint to receive incoming messages from WhatsApp.
    '''
    data = request.json
    if 'messages' in data:
        for message in data['messages']:
            incoming_text = message['text']['body']
            sender = message['from']
            response_text = whatsapp_api.receive_message(incoming_text)
            whatsapp_api.send_message(sender, response_text)
    return "Webhook received", 200
```

```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from flask import Flask, request
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI

class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"

    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")

    def receive_message(self, incoming_message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        incoming_message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(incoming_message)
        return response

# Flask app for webhook
app = Flask(__name__)
whatsapp_api = WhatsAppAPI(phone_number_id=os.getenv("WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"))

@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])
def webhook():
    '''
    Webhook endpoint to receive incoming messages from WhatsApp.
    '''
    data = request.json
    if 'messages' in data:
        for message in data['messages']:
            incoming_text = message['text']['body']
            sender = message['from']
            response_text = whatsapp_api.receive_message(incoming_text)
            whatsapp_api.send_message(sender, response_text)
    return "Webhook received", 200
```

```python
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO customers (name, phone) VALUES (?, ?)
        ''', (customer_data['name'], customer_data['phone']))
        self.connection.commit()

    def book_service(self, booking_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)
        ''', (booking_data['customer_id'], booking_data['service'], booking_data['date']))
        self.connection.commit()

    def get_bookings(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM bookings')
        return cursor.fetchall()
```

notifications.py
```python
'''
Handles notification features for the application.
'''
import os
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart

class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.smtp_server = os.getenv("SMTP_SERVER")
        self.smtp_port = os.getenv("SMTP_PORT")
        self.smtp_user = os.getenv("SMTP_USER")
        self.smtp_password = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD")

    def send_notification(self, user_email, subject, message):
        '''
        Sends a notification to the specified user with the given message.
        Parameters:
        user_email (str): The recipient's email address.
        subject (str): The subject of the email.
        message (str): The message content of the email.
        '''
        try:
            # Set up the server
            server = smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port)
            server.starttls()
            server.login(self.smtp_user, self.smtp_password)
            # Create the email
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.smtp_user
            msg['To'] = user_email
            msg['Subject'] = subject
            msg.attach(MIMEText(message, 'plain'))
            # Send the email
            server.sendmail(self.smtp_user, user_email, msg.as_string())
            server.quit()
            print(f"Notification sent to {user_email}: {subject}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send notification: {e}")
```

whatsapp_api.py
```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from flask import Flask, request
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI
class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"
    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")
    def receive_message(self, incoming_message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        incoming_message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(incoming_message)
        return response
# Flask app for webhook
app = Flask(__name__)
whatsapp_api = WhatsAppAPI(phone_number_id=os.getenv("WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"))
@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])
def webhook():
    '''
    Webhook endpoint to receive incoming messages from WhatsApp.
    '''
    data = request.json
    if 'messages' in data:
        for message in data['messages']:
            incoming_text = message['text']['body']
            sender = message['from']
            response_text = whatsapp_api.receive_message(incoming_text)
            whatsapp_api.send_message(sender, response_text)
    return "Webhook received", 200
```

chatgpt_api.py
```python
'''
Interfaces with the OpenAI ChatGPT API for intelligent conversation.
'''
import os
import openai
class ChatGPTAPI:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        '''
        Initializes the ChatGPTAPI with the provided OpenAI API key.
        Parameters:
        api_key (str): The API key for authenticating with OpenAI.
        '''
        self.api_key = api_key
        openai.api_key = self.api_key
    def get_response(self, prompt):
        '''
        Gets a response from the ChatGPT model based on the provided prompt.
        Parameters:
        prompt (str): The input text to which the model should respond.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by the ChatGPT model.
        '''
        try:
            response = openai.Completion.create(
                engine="text-davinci-003",
                prompt=prompt,
                max_tokens=150
            )
            return response.choices[0].text.strip()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to get response from ChatGPT: {e}")
            return "Sorry, I'm having trouble understanding you right now."
```

database.py
```python
'''
Manages database operations for customer registration and booking.
'''
import sqlite3
class DatabaseManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.connection = sqlite3.connect('chatbot.db')
        self.create_tables()
    def create_tables(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                phone TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER,
                service TEXT NOT NULL,
                date TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)
            )
        ''')
        self.connection.commit()
    def register_customer(self, customer_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO customers (name, phone) VALUES (?, ?)
        ''', (customer_data['name'], customer_data['phone']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def book_service(self, booking_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)
        ''', (booking_data['customer_id'], booking_data['service'], booking_data['date']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def get_bookings(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM bookings')
        return cursor.fetchall()
```

notifications.py
```python
'''
Handles notification features for the application.
'''
import os
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.smtp_server = os.getenv("SMTP_SERVER")
        self.smtp_port = os.getenv("SMTP_PORT")
        self.smtp_user = os.getenv("SMTP_USER")
        self.smtp_password = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD")
    def send_notification(self, user_email, subject, message):
        '''
        Sends a notification to the specified user with the given message.
        Parameters:
        user_email (str): The recipient's email address.
        subject (str): The subject of the email.
        message (str): The message content of the email.
        '''
        try:
            # Set up the server
            server = smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port)
            server.starttls()
            server.login(self.smtp_user, self.smtp_password)
            # Create the email
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.smtp_user
            msg['To'] = user_email
            msg['Subject'] = subject
            msg.attach(MIMEText(message, 'plain'))
            # Send the email
            server.sendmail(self.smtp_user, user_email, msg.as_string())
            server.quit()
            print(f"Notification sent to {user_email}: {subject}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send notification: {e}")
```

```python
    def __init__(self, hostinger_credentials):
        self.hostinger_credentials = hostinger_credentials
    def deploy_application(self):
        '''
        Deploys the application to HOSTINGER using the provided credentials.
        '''
        # Simulate deployment process
        print("Starting deployment to HOSTINGER...")
        # Example: Using subprocess to run deployment commands
        try:
            # This is a placeholder for actual deployment commands
            subprocess.run(["echo", "Deploying application..."], check=True)
            print("Application deployed successfully on HOSTINGER.")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print(f"Deployment failed: {e}")
```

whatsapp_api.py
```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from flask import Flask, request
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI
class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"
    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")
    def receive_message(self, incoming_message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        incoming_message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(incoming_message)
        return response
# Flask app for webhook
app = Flask(__name__)
whatsapp_api = WhatsAppAPI(phone_number_id=os.getenv("WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"))
@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])
def webhook():
    '''
    Webhook endpoint to receive incoming messages from WhatsApp.
    '''
    data = request.json
    if 'messages' in data:
        for message in data['messages']:
            incoming_text = message['text']['body']
            sender = message['from']
            response_text = whatsapp_api.receive_message(incoming_text)
            whatsapp_api.send_message(sender, response_text)
    return "Webhook received", 200
```
chatgpt_api.py
```python
'''
Interfaces with the OpenAI ChatGPT API for intelligent conversation.
'''
import os
import openai
class ChatGPTAPI:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        '''
        Initializes the ChatGPTAPI with the provided OpenAI API key.
        Parameters:
        api_key (str): The API key for authenticating with OpenAI.
        '''
        self.api_key = api_key
        openai.api_key = self.api_key
    def get_response(self, prompt):
        '''
        Gets a response from the ChatGPT model based on the provided prompt.
        Parameters:
        prompt (str): The input text to which the model should respond.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by the ChatGPT model.
        '''
        try:
            response = openai.Completion.create(
                engine="text-davinci-003",
                prompt=prompt,
                max_tokens=150
            )
            return response.choices[0].text.strip()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to get response from ChatGPT: {e}")
            return "Sorry, I'm having trouble understanding you right now."
```
database.py
```python
'''
Manages database operations for customer registration and booking.
'''
import sqlite3
class DatabaseManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.connection = sqlite3.connect('chatbot.db')
        self.create_tables()
    def create_tables(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                phone TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER,
                service TEXT NOT NULL,
                date TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)
            )
        ''')
        self.connection.commit()
    def register_customer(self, customer_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO customers (name, phone) VALUES (?, ?)
        ''', (customer_data['name'], customer_data['phone']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def book_service(self, booking_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)
        ''', (booking_data['customer_id'], booking_data['service'], booking_data['date']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def get_bookings(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM bookings')
        return cursor.fetchall()
```
notifications.py
```python
'''
Handles notification features for the application.
'''
import os
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.smtp_server = os.getenv("SMTP_SERVER")
        self.smtp_port = os.getenv("SMTP_PORT")
        self.smtp_user = os.getenv("SMTP_USER")
        self.smtp_password = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD")
    def send_notification(self, user_email, subject, message):
        '''
        Sends a notification to the specified user with the given message.
        Parameters:
        user_email (str): The recipient's email address.
        subject (str): The subject of the email.
        message (str): The message content of the email.
        '''
        try:
            # Set up the server
            server = smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port)
            server.starttls()
            server.login(self.smtp_user, self.smtp_password)
            # Create the email
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.smtp_user
            msg['To'] = user_email
            msg['Subject'] = subject
            msg.attach(MIMEText(message, 'plain'))
            # Send the email
            server.sendmail(self.smtp_user, user_email, msg.as_string())
            server.quit()
            print(f"Notification sent to {user_email}: {subject}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send notification: {e}")
```

```python
class DeploymentManager:
    def __init__(self, hostinger_credentials):
        self.hostinger_credentials = hostinger_credentials
    def deploy_application(self):
        '''
        Deploys the application to HOSTINGER using the provided credentials.
        '''

        print("Starting deployment to HOSTINGER...")
        # Example: Using subprocess to run deployment commands
        try:
            # This is a placeholder for actual deployment commands
            subprocess.run(["echo", "Deploying application..."], check=True)
            print("Application deployed successfully on HOSTINGER.")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print(f"Deployment failed: {e}")
```

whatsapp_api.py
```python
'''
Manages interactions with the Meta Cloud API for WhatsApp messaging.
'''
import os
import requests
from flask import Flask, request
from chatgpt_api import ChatGPTAPI
class WhatsAppAPI:
    def __init__(self, phone_number_id):
        '''
        Initializes the WhatsAppAPI with the provided API keys and phone number ID.
        Parameters:
        phone_number_id (str): The phone number ID for sending messages.
        '''
        self.api_key = os.getenv("WHATSAPP_API_KEY")
        self.chatgpt = ChatGPTAPI(os.getenv("CHATGPT_API_KEY"))
        self.phone_number_id = phone_number_id
        self.base_url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v13.0/{self.phone_number_id}/messages"
    def send_message(self, recipient, message):
        '''
        Sends a message via WhatsApp API.
        Parameters:
        recipient (str): The recipient's phone number.
        message (str): The message text to send.
        '''
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        data = {
            "messaging_product": "whatsapp",
            "to": recipient,
            "text": {"body": message}
        }
        try:
            response = requests.post(self.base_url, headers=headers, json=data)
            response.raise_for_status()
            print(f"Message sent to {recipient}: {message}")
        except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
            print(f"Failed to send message: {e}")
    def receive_message(self, incoming_message):
        '''
        Handles incoming messages and generates a response using ChatGPT.
        Parameters:
        incoming_message (str): The incoming message text.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by ChatGPT.
        '''
        response = self.chatgpt.get_response(incoming_message)
        return response
# Flask app for webhook
app = Flask(__name__)
whatsapp_api = WhatsAppAPI(phone_number_id=os.getenv("WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID"))
@app.route('/webhook', methods=['POST'])
def webhook():
    '''
    Webhook endpoint to receive incoming messages from WhatsApp.
    '''
    data = request.json
    if 'messages' in data:
        for message in data['messages']:
            incoming_text = message['text']['body']
            sender = message['from']
            response_text = whatsapp_api.receive_message(incoming_text)
            whatsapp_api.send_message(sender, response_text)
    return "Webhook received", 200
```

chatgpt_api.py
```python
'''
Interfaces with the OpenAI ChatGPT API for intelligent conversation.
'''
import os
import openai
class ChatGPTAPI:
    def __init__(self, api_key):
        '''
        Initializes the ChatGPTAPI with the provided OpenAI API key.
        Parameters:
        api_key (str): The API key for authenticating with OpenAI.
        '''
        self.api_key = api_key
        openai.api_key = self.api_key
    def get_response(self, prompt):
        '''
        Gets a response from the ChatGPT model based on the provided prompt.
        Parameters:
        prompt (str): The input text to which the model should respond.
        Returns:
        str: The response generated by the ChatGPT model.
        '''
        try:
            response = openai.Completion.create(
                engine="text-davinci-003",
                prompt=prompt,
                max_tokens=150
            )
            return response.choices[0].text.strip()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to get response from ChatGPT: {e}")
            return "Sorry, I'm having trouble understanding you right now."
```

database.py
```python
'''
Manages database operations for customer registration and booking.
'''
import sqlite3
class DatabaseManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.connection = sqlite3.connect('chatbot.db')
        self.create_tables()
    def create_tables(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS customers (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                phone TEXT NOT NULL
            )
        ''')
        cursor.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bookings (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                customer_id INTEGER,
                service TEXT NOT NULL,
                date TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(customer_id) REFERENCES customers(id)
            )
        ''')
        self.connection.commit()
    def register_customer(self, customer_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO customers (name, phone) VALUES (?, ?)
        ''', (customer_data['name'], customer_data['phone']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def book_service(self, booking_data):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('''
            INSERT INTO bookings (customer_id, service, date) VALUES (?, ?, ?)
        ''', (booking_data['customer_id'], booking_data['service'], booking_data['date']))
        self.connection.commit()
    def get_bookings(self):
        cursor = self.connection.cursor()
        cursor.execute('SELECT * FROM bookings')
        return cursor.fetchall()
```

notifications.py
```python
'''
Handles notification features for the application.
'''
import os
import smtplib
from email.mime.text import MIMEText
from email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart
class NotificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.smtp_server = os.getenv("SMTP_SERVER")
        self.smtp_port = os.getenv("SMTP_PORT")
        self.smtp_user = os.getenv("SMTP_USER")
        self.smtp_password = os.getenv("SMTP_PASSWORD")
    def send_notification(self, user_email, subject, message):
        '''
        Sends a notification to the specified user with the given message.
        Parameters:
        user_email (str): The recipient's email address.
        subject (str): The subject of the email.
        message (str): The message content of the email.
        '''
        try:
            # Set up the server
            server = smtplib.SMTP(self.smtp_server, self.smtp_port)
            server.starttls()
            server.login(self.smtp_user, self.smtp_password)
            # Create the email
            msg = MIMEMultipart()
            msg['From'] = self.smtp_user
            msg['To'] = user_email
            msg['Subject'] = subject
            msg.attach(MIMEText(message, 'plain'))
            # Send the email
            server.sendmail(self.smtp_user, user_email, msg.as_string())
            server.quit()
            print(f"Notification sent to {user_email}: {subject}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to send notification: {e}")
```

```python
'''
Handles deployment of the application on HOSTINGER.
'''
import subprocess
class DeploymentManager:
    def __init__(self, hostinger_credentials):
        self.hostinger_credentials = hostinger_credentials
    def deploy_application(self):
        '''
        Deploys the application to HOSTINGER using the provided credentials.
        '''
        # Simulate deployment process
        print("Starting deployment to HOSTINGER...")
        # Example: Using subprocess to run deployment commands
        try:
            # This is a placeholder for actual deployment commands
            subprocess.run(["echo", "Deploying application..."], check=True)
            print("Application deployed successfully on HOSTINGER.")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print(f"Deployment failed: {e}")
```

```
# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)
```

# WhatsApp Chatbot with Meta Cloud API and OpenAI ChatGPT

This user manual provides detailed instructions on how to use the WhatsApp Chatbot application integrated with Meta Cloud API for messaging and OpenAI ChatGPT API for intelligent conversation. The application includes customer registration, service booking flows, an admin dashboard for managing bookings, and notification features, all backed by a database and deployed on HOSTINGER.

## Main Functions

### 1. WhatsApp Messaging
- **Send and Receive Messages**: The application uses Meta Cloud API to send and receive messages via WhatsApp.
- **Intelligent Conversation**: OpenAI's ChatGPT API is integrated to provide intelligent responses to incoming messages.

### 2. Customer Registration and Service Booking
- **Customer Registration**: Users can register their details, which are stored in a database.
- **Service Booking**: Customers can book services, and these bookings are managed within the application.

### 3. Admin Dashboard
- **Manage Bookings**: An admin dashboard is provided to view and manage customer bookings.
- **Graphical User Interface**: The dashboard is built using Tkinter for easy interaction.

### 4. Notifications
- **Email Notifications**: The application can send email notifications to users regarding their bookings and other updates.

### 5. Deployment
- **Deploy on HOSTINGER**: The application is designed to be deployed on HOSTINGER, ensuring it is accessible and operational.

## Installation

### Environment Setup

1. **Clone the Repository**: Clone the application repository to your local machine.
   ```bash
   git clone <repository-url>
   ```

2. **Install Dependencies**: Install the required Python packages using pip.
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. **Environment Variables**: Set up environment variables for API keys and HOSTINGER credentials. Create a `.env` file in the root directory and add the following:
   ```
   WHATSAPP_API_KEY=<your-whatsapp-api-key>
   CHATGPT_API_KEY=<your-chatgpt-api-key>
   HOSTINGER_USERNAME=<your-hostinger-username>
   HOSTINGER_PASSWORD=<your-hostinger-password>
   SMTP_SERVER=<your-smtp-server>
   SMTP_PORT=<your-smtp-port>
   SMTP_USER=<your-smtp-user>
   SMTP_PASSWORD=<your-smtp-password>
   WHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID=<your-whatsapp-phone-number-id>
   ```

### Database Setup

1. **SQLite Database**: The application uses SQLite for database operations. Ensure SQLite is installed on your system.

2. **Initialize Database**: Run the application once to initialize the database and create necessary tables.

## Usage

### Running the Application

1. **Start the Flask Server**: Run the Flask server to handle incoming WhatsApp messages.
   ```bash
   python whatsapp_api.py
   ```

2. **Launch Admin Dashboard**: Open the admin dashboard to manage bookings.
   ```bash
   python gui.py
   ```

### Deployment

1. **Deploy on HOSTINGER**: Use the deployment script to deploy the application on HOSTINGER.
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

### Notifications

1. **Send Notifications**: Use the notification manager to send email notifications to users.
   ```python
   from notifications import NotificationManager
   notification_manager = NotificationManager()
   notification_manager.send_notification(user_email, subject, message)
   ```

## Documentation

For further documentation and support, please refer to the application's repository or contact the development team.

```

This manual provides a comprehensive guide to installing, configuring, and using the WhatsApp Chatbot application. It covers all necessary steps from environment setup to deployment and usage, ensuring users can effectively utilize the software's features.
```
